==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [ssrf] Possible SSRF (Server Side Request Forgery) vulnerability.
Severity: HIGH
Description: The configuration may allow attacker to create a arbitrary requests from the vulnerable server.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/ssrf.md
Reason: At least variable "$1" can contain untrusted user input
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name localhost;

	location ~ ^/services/(.*)/1(.*)$ {
		proxy_pass http://$1/services/$1/1$2$is_args$args;
	}
}

>> Problem: [alias_traversal] Path traversal via misconfigured alias.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: Using alias in a prefixed location that doesn't ends with directory separator could lead to path traversal vulnerability.

server {
	server_name _;

	location /content {
		alias /opt/graphite/webapp/content;
	}

	location /media {
		alias /usr/share/pyshared/django/contrib/admin/media;
	}
}

./scrapes/jfelege/todo-app/master/todo-vagrant/nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [origins] Validation regex for "origin" or "referrer" matches untrusted domain.
Severity: HIGH
Description: Improve the regular expression to match only trusted referrers.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/origins.md
Reason: Regex matches "http://evil.com/http://159/203/96/110.evil.com", "http://evil.com/https://159/203/96/110.evil.com", "http://evil.com/https://localhost.evil.com", "http://evil.com/http://localhost.evil.com" as a valid origin.
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name localhost;

	location /api/ {

		if ($http_origin ~* https?://(localhost|159.203.96.110)) {
		}
	}
}

>> Problem: [alias_traversal] Path traversal via misconfigured alias.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: Using alias in a prefixed location that doesn't ends with directory separator could lead to path traversal vulnerability.

Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name .$hostname.ru .$hostname.com;

		alias /data/inernal;
	}

	location /media {
		alias /data/media;
	}

	location /static {
		alias /data/static;
	}
}

./scrapes/gszathmari/sritest-frontend/master/nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [add_header_redefinition] Nested "add_header" drops parent headers.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: "add_header" replaces ALL parent headers. See documentation: http://nginx.org/en/docs/http/ngx_http_headers_module.html#add_header
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/addheaderredefinition.md
Reason: Parent headers "x-content-type-options", "x-xss-protection", "x-frame-options" was dropped in current level
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name localhost;
	add_header X-Frame-Options DENY;
	add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff;
	add_header X-XSS-Protection 1; mode=block;
	add_header Content-Security-Policy-Report-Only img-src 'self' www.google-analytics.com heapanalytics.com pixel.quantserve.com; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' 'unsafe-eval' in.getclicky.com cdn.mxpnl.com secure.quantserve.com js-agent.newrelic.com bam.nr-data.net api.keen.io cdn.heapanalytics.com static.getclicky.com www.google.com ajax.googleapis.com ajax.cloudflare.com www.googletagmanager.com *.cloudfront.net www.google-analytics.com cdn.segment.com; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' www.google.com fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' data: fonts.gstatic.com; connect-src 'self' api.mixpanel.com api.segment.io api.sritest.io; report-uri https://report-uri.io/report/sritest/reportOnly;
	add_header Strict-Transport-Security max-age=31536000; includeSubdomains; preload;

	location ~* \.(?:jpg|jpeg|gif|png|ico|cur|gz|svg|svgz|mp4|ogg|ogv|webm|htc)$ {
		add_header Cache-Control public;
	}

	location ~* \.(?:css|js)$ {
		add_header Cache-Control public;
	}

	location ~* \.(?:ttf|ttc|otf|eot|woff|woff2)$ {
		add_header Cache-Control public;
	}
}

Pseudo config:

server {

	location /media {
		alias /var/www/html/media;
	}

	location /static {
		alias /var/www/html/static;
	}
}

	location /media/book {
		alias /home/book/bookspider/booksite/bookstore/book;

	}
}

./scrapes/plainblack/Wing/master/var/init/nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [add_header_redefinition] Nested "add_header" drops parent headers.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: "add_header" replaces ALL parent headers. See documentation: http://nginx.org/en/docs/http/ngx_http_headers_module.html#add_header
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/addheaderredefinition.md
Reason: Parent headers "x-frame-options", "x-xss-protection", "x-content-type-options" was dropped in current level
Pseudo config:
add_header X-XSS-Protection 1;
add_header X-Frame-Options SAMEORIGIN;
add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff;

server {
	server_name localhost;

	location ~ \.(html|xml|txt|json) {
		add_header Cache-Control must-revalidate;
		add_header Cache-Control public;
		add_header Access-Control-Allow-Origin *;
	}
}

>> Problem: [host_spoofing] The proxied Host header may be spoofed.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: In most cases "$host" variable are more appropriate, just use it.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/hostspoofing.md
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name localhost;

	location ^~ /crawler {
		proxy_set_header Host $http_host;
	}

	location / {
		proxy_set_header Host $http_host;
	}

	location /api {
		proxy_set_header Host $http_host;
	}
}

./scrapes/dawnbreak/hubzilla/master/sample-nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [http_splitting] Possible HTTP-Splitting vulnerability.
Severity: HIGH
Description: Using variables that can contain "\n" or "\r" may lead to http injection.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/httpsplitting.md
Reason: At least variable "$uri" can contain "\n"
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name red.example.net;

	location / {

		if ($is_args != ) {
			rewrite ^/(.*) /index.php?q=$uri&$args last;
		}
		rewrite ^/(.*) /index.php?q=$uri last;
	}

	location ^~ /.well-known/ {
		rewrite ^/(.*) /index.php?q=$uri&$args last;
	}
}

server {
	server_name red.example.net;

	location / {

		if ($is_args != ) {

		}
		rewrite ^/(.*) /index.php?q=$uri last;
	}

	location ^~ /.well-known/ {
		rewrite ^/(.*) /index.php?q=$uri&$args last;
	}
}

./scrapes/ZWS2014/freebsdashboard/master/static/DefaultConfigFiles/nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [add_header_redefinition] Nested "add_header" drops parent headers.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: "add_header" replaces ALL parent headers. See documentation: http://nginx.org/en/docs/http/ngx_http_headers_module.html#add_header
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/addheaderredefinition.md
Reason: Parent headers "x-frame-options" was dropped in current level
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name _;
	add_header X-Frame-Options SAMEORIGIN;

	location ~* \.(jpg|jpeg|png|gif|ico|css|js)$ {
		add_header Pragma public;
		add_header Cache-Control public, must-revalidate, proxy-revalidate;
	}
}

------------------------------------------------

>> Problem: [alias_traversal] Path traversal via misconfigured alias.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: Using alias in a prefixed location that doesn't ends with directory separator could lead to path traversal vulnerability. 
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/aliastraversal.md
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name _;

	location /media {
		alias /usr/local/freebsdashboard/web/media;
	}

	location /static {
		alias /usr/local/freebsdashboard/web/static;
	}
}

==================== Summary ===================
Total issues:
    Unspecified: 0
    Low: 0
    Medium: 3
    High: 0

./scrapes/hlcfan/pokr/master/nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [add_header_redefinition] Nested "add_header" drops parent headers.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: "add_header" replaces ALL parent headers. See documentation: http://nginx.org/en/docs/http/ngx_http_headers_module.html#add_header
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/addheaderredefinition.md
Reason: Parent headers "x-content-type-options", "x-frame-options" was dropped in current level
Pseudo config:

server {
	add_header X-Frame-Options SAMEORIGIN;
	add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff;

	location ~ ^/(assets)/ {
		add_header Cache-Control public;
		add_header Last-Modified ;
		add_header ETag ;
	}

	location ~ .*\.(gif|jpg|jpeg|png|bmp|ico|txt|xml|html)$ {
		add_header Cache-Control public;
	}
}

------------------------------------------------

>> Problem: [host_spoofing] The proxied Host header may be spoofed.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: In most cases "$host" variable are more appropriate, just use it.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/hostspoofing.md
Pseudo config:

server {

	location / {
		proxy_set_header Host $http_host;
	}

	location ^~ /cable {
		proxy_set_header Host $http_host;
	}
}

Severity: MEDIUM
Description: Using alias in a prefixed location that doesn't ends with directory separator could lead to path traversal vulnerability.

./scrapes/xtrafrancyz/vk-proxy/master/nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [ssrf] Possible SSRF (Server Side Request Forgery) vulnerability.
Severity: HIGH
Description: The configuration may allow attacker to create a arbitrary requests from the vulnerable server.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/ssrf.md
Reason: At least variable "$1" can contain untrusted user input
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name vk-api-proxy.example.com;

	location /_ {

		location ~ ^/_/(?:vk\.com|(?:[-_a-zA-Z0-9]+)\.(?:userapi\.com|vk-cdn\.net|vk\.(?:me|com)|mycdn\.me|vkuser(?:live|video|audio|)\.(?:net|com)))/ {
			rewrite /_/([^/]+)/(.*) /$2 break;
			proxy_pass https://$1;
		}
	}
}

==================== Summary ===================

    Unspecified: 0
    Low: 0
    Medium: 0
    High: 1

./scrapes/concurrentlabs/laguna/master/1.0/scripts/nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [http_splitting] Possible HTTP-Splitting vulnerability.
Severity: HIGH
Description: Using variables that can contain "\n" or "\r" may lead to http injection.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/httpsplitting.md
Reason: At least variable "$ccurourl" can contain "\r"
Pseudo config:

server {

	location /ccur/ {

		location ~ (?P<ccursvc>^/ccur(/[^/]*)*)/tcshost/(?P<ccurhost>[^/]+)/tcskey(?P<ccurid>/[^/]+)(?P<ccurmisc>/[^/]+)/tcsopt/(?P<ccuropt>[^/]+)/tcsosig(?P<ccurourl>/.+)$ {
			rewrite ^.*$ $ccurourl break;
		}
	}
}

------------------------------------------------

>> Problem: [http_splitting] Possible HTTP-Splitting vulnerability.
Severity: HIGH
Description: Using variables that can contain "\n" or "\r" may lead to http injection.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/httpsplitting.md
Reason: At least variable "$ccurhost" can contain "\n"
Pseudo config:

server {

	location /ccur/ {

		location ~ (?P<ccursvc>^/ccur(/[^/]*)*)/tcshost/(?P<ccurhost>[^/]+)/tcskey(?P<ccurid>/[^/]+)(?P<ccurmisc>/[^/]+)/tcsopt/(?P<ccuropt>[^/]+)/tcsosig(?P<ccurourl>/.+)$ {
			proxy_pass http://$ccurhost;
		}
	}
}

------------------------------------------------

>> Problem: [ssrf] Possible SSRF (Server Side Request Forgery) vulnerability.
Severity: HIGH
Description: The configuration may allow attacker to create a arbitrary requests from the vulnerable server.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/ssrf.md
Reason: At least variable "$ccurhost" can contain untrusted user input
Pseudo config:

server {

	location /ccur/ {

		location ~ (?P<ccursvc>^/ccur(/[^/]*)*)/tcshost/(?P<ccurhost>[^/]+)/tcskey(?P<ccurid>/[^/]+)(?P<ccurmisc>/[^/]+)/tcsopt/(?P<ccuropt>[^/]+)/tcsosig(?P<ccurourl>/.+)$ {
			proxy_pass http://$ccurhost;
		}
	}
}

==================== Summary ===================
Total issues:
    Unspecified: 0
    Low: 0
    Medium: 0
    High: 3

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [alias_traversal] Path traversal via misconfigured alias.
Severity: HIGH
Description: Using alias in a prefixed location that doesn't ends with directory separator could lead to path traversal vulnerability. 
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/aliastraversal.md
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name localhost;

	location /static {
		alias /usr/share/nginx/html/static/;
	}
}

------------------------------------------------

>> Problem: [add_header_redefinition] Nested "add_header" drops parent headers.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: "add_header" replaces ALL parent headers. See documentation: http://nginx.org/en/docs/http/ngx_http_headers_module.html#add_header
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/addheaderredefinition.md
Reason: Parent headers "x-content-type-options", "x-frame-options", "x-xss-protection" was dropped in current level
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name localhost;
	add_header X-Frame-Options SAMEORIGIN;
	add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff;
	add_header X-XSS-Protection 1; mode=block;
	add_header Strict-Transport-Security max-age=31536000; includeSubdomains;;
	add_header Referrer-Policy no-referrer-when-downgrade;

	location / {
		add_header Cache-Control no-store, no-cache, must-revalidate;
	}

	location /static {
		add_header Cache-Control public;
	}
}

    Unspecified: 0
    Low: 0
    Medium: 2
    High: 1

./scrapes/lunared/ftmp3/nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [http_splitting] Possible HTTP-Splitting vulnerability.
Severity: HIGH
Description: Using variables that can contain "\n" or "\r" may lead to http injection.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/httpsplitting.md
Reason: At least variable "$request_basename" can contain "\n"
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name web;

	location ~ ^.*/(?P<request_basename>[^/]+\.(mp3|ogg|midi|mid))$ {
		add_header Content-Disposition attachment; filename="$request_basename";
	}
}

------------------------------------------------

>> Problem: [add_header_redefinition] Nested "add_header" drops parent headers.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: "add_header" replaces ALL parent headers. See documentation: http://nginx.org/en/docs/http/ngx_http_headers_module.html#add_header
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/addheaderredefinition.md
Reason: Parent headers "x-content-type-options" was dropped in current level
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name web;
	add_header Strict-Transport-Security max-age=63072000; includeSubdomains; preload;
	add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff;

	location ~ (?P<request_basename>^.*\.(mp3|ogg|midi|mid))/stream$ {
		add_header Accept-Ranges bytes;
	}

	location ~ ^.*/(?P<request_basename>[^/]+\.(mp3|ogg|midi|mid))$ {
		add_header Content-Disposition attachment; filename="$request_basename";
	}
}

------------------------------------------------

>> Problem: [host_spoofing] The proxied Host header may be spoofed.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: In most cases "$host" variable are more appropriate, just use it.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/hostspoofing.md
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name web;

	location / {
		proxy_set_header Host $http_host;
	}
}

==================== Summary ===================
Total issues:
    Unspecified: 0
    Low: 0
    Medium: 3
    High: 1

./scrapes/leoandshaw/go9999.com/master/nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [http_splitting] Possible HTTP-Splitting vulnerability.
Severity: HIGH
Description: Using variables that can contain "\n" or "\r" may lead to http injection.
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/httpsplitting.md
Reason: At least variable "$uri" can contain "\n"
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name www.go9999.com;

	location / {

		if (!-f $request_filename) {
			rewrite .* /index.php?q=$uri&$args;
		}

		location ~ \.php$ {

			if (!-f $request_filename) {
				rewrite .* /index.php?q=$uri&$args;
			}
		}
	}
}

==================== Summary ===================
Total issues:
    Unspecified: 0
    Low: 0
    Medium: 0
    High: 2

./scrapes/rwth-acis/mobsos-survey/master/etc/nginx.conf

==================== Results ===================

>> Problem: [add_header_redefinition] Nested "add_header" drops parent headers.
Severity: MEDIUM
Description: "add_header" replaces ALL parent headers. See documentation: http://nginx.org/en/docs/http/ngx_http_headers_module.html#add_header
Additional info: https://github.com/yandex/gixy/blob/master/docs/en/plugins/addheaderredefinition.md
Reason: Parent headers "cache-control" was dropped in current level
Pseudo config:

server {
	server_name localhost;

	location / {
		add_header Cache-Control max-age=31536000;

		if ($request_method = OPTIONS) {
			add_header Access-Control-Allow-Origin *;
			add_header Access-Control-Allow-Methods GET, POST, OPTIONS;
			add_header Access-Control-Allow-Headers DNT,User-Agent,X-Requested-With,If-Modified-Since,Cache-Control,Content-Type,Range;
			add_header Access-Control-Max-Age 1728000;
			add_header Content-Type text/plain; charset=utf-8;
			add_header Content-Length 0;
		}

		if ($request_method = POST) {
			add_header Access-Control-Allow-Origin *;
			add_header Access-Control-Allow-Methods GET, POST, OPTIONS;
			add_header Access-Control-Allow-Headers DNT,User-Agent,X-Requested-With,If-Modified-Since,Cache-Control,Content-Type,Range;
			add_header Access-Control-Expose-Headers Content-Length,Content-Range;
		}

		if ($request_method = GET) {
			add_header Access-Control-Allow-Origin *;
			add_header Access-Control-Allow-Methods GET, POST, OPTIONS;
			add_header Access-Control-Allow-Headers DNT,User-Agent,X-Requested-With,If-Modified-Since,Cache-Control,Content-Type,Range;
			add_header Access-Control-Expose-Headers Content-Length,Content-Range;
		}
	}
}

==================== Summary ===================
Total issues:
    Unspecified: 0
    Low: 0
    Medium: 3
    High: 0
